<user_id>116726288586888214835</user_id>< user_name>
Frank Vuong<//user_name>
< time>
1553465372929</time>
<Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
You can't beat the house special noodle. The main Hủ Tiếu Thanh Xuân is originated from Mỹ Tho, (a.k.a hủ tiếu Mỹ Tho), a uniquely deep-southwestern Vietnamese noodle.

Order the Dry version where they put the broth on the side instead of in the noodle.  The dry version comes Also with a special shrimp sauce on the side for you to pour into you nood bowl.  You can eat it dry like stir fry or pour the broth in and eat like a nooodle soup.  This brings out the unique southwesteen Vietnamese nooddle.  Be sure to order the "clear noodle" for an even more authentic taste.

DO NOT compare the hủ tiếu here with the ones at Chinese restaurants. At the Chinese restaurant they may use the same noodle but their broth is for "mì" which is egg-noodle and it is totally wrong.

The Hủ Tiếu here is "supposed" to taste light and fresh, much different than the Chinese noodles which tend to be heavily flavored.  It also comes with fresh bean sprout.  It also authentically comes with "rau tần ô" (
garland chrysanthemum,[5]chrysanthemum greens,[5] edible chrysanthemum, crowndaisy chrysanthemum,[6] chop suey green,[5] crown daisy,[5] "

If your southwestern noodle doesn't come with "rau tần ô", then its a totally different type of noodle soup.  More often than not, at another restaurant, you will be eating some weird fusion noodle that doesn't originate anywhere but from the chefs mind for convenience sake and not authentic.

The price is ridiculously cheap.  A small bowl for under $5 compared to other noodle places that can go up to $8, albeit the portion is slightly smaller but still satisfying without the bloated feeling afterwards.

I started going here 30 years ago and now, although there has been a change in ownership, the same authentic freshness is still there.  Perhaps the same chef remains.

Oh, and you get a free "nước mát" which is yet another freshly sweet drink.

With such a cheap meal, please tip them generously.< /Text>

< Review>
I’ve been here twice and enjoyed the experience each time. Pizzas are made to order and their ingredients are fresh!  The crust is amazing and has such good texture/taste.  You order and pay at the counter, then they bring your pizza to you.  It’s a bit odd and inconvenient that you have to get your own utensils, napkins, and condiments (quality Parmesan, chili flakes, oil, honey, etc.), especially if you’re sitting on the other end of the restaurant.  Maybe they have that setup so they can keep their prices so low, in which case I don’t mind at all!

You can’t really go wrong with any pizza on their menu but I especially enjoyed the prosciutto truffle pizza.

Parking: the first hour is free. $1 for every 30 minutes after that.  Service is so fast here that you won’t need more than an hour!< /Review>

Eventhrough we told him it was the wrong item. He kept insisting it was the right one. So we told him to check the price and the item number and we have even showed him the receipt with the item description. The other staffs were still busy chatting with each other. So he was all by himself, despite our insisting he still said this is the right item. In the end we showed him all the evidence we have and he couldn’t deny it and said he will look inside again and this time he came back with the right item.
We truelly hope it was just a mistake and not some scamm to trick the costumers. The usually friendly welcome and professional service are undoubtly missing in this shop.<//Text>< Rating>

We took it to xtreme auto because the mechanic recommended by allstate was closed at the time of the incident. They towed it free-of-charge for being less than a mile away and checked in with us every tuesday and thursday to keep us updated on the progress. <rating>5< /rating><Review>Update 9/9/2020 Play with Orange Sky Covid-19
Since COVID-19 opening on this golf course, the price has gone up, haven't played here often. Yesterday, my friend booked online special for $38 per person walking, so we went. It happened to have Orange Sky due to fire smoke everywhere, but the air was quite nice and the grass was actually wet. We really like this golf course, it's quite long for us short distance players but it's well kept even with COVID-19. One little problem, MOSQUITOS are everywhere and we did get bit LOL.
I added some pictures of the whole golf course with orange sky but hole #11. I used the SwingU software which is quite nice for GPS distance and map, although the distance was not extremely accurate but we're not that precise ourselves so it's OK.

Update 10/2/19
For $23-28 round of walking, this golf course now is the best so far in the bay area. I went in through the entrance where the guard was extremely hostile last time to meet a very courteous and pleasant one this time, what a great improvement I thought.
The golf course is green and beautiful. I and my friends were amazed at the fairway, the grass is so nice and green, we felt like we're walking on carpet, the soil is soft and grass is thick. It's only 6300-6600 yards dependent upon white to blue but it's quite challenging. We're all agreed that it's much better than Shorelines, soon to be gone Santa Clara and SJ muni. It was a Weds afternoon, we could finish the round in 4 hours. The sand traps are every where around the greens but the sands are easy to play, plenty of them. Yes, it's quite windy in some holes like the Shorelines.
The greens are well taken care and extremely fast IMHO, I had 3 putted greens quite easily.
Some narrow fairways and quite a few doglegged right and left which make the golf course very challenging. The more holes we played the more we're impressed with the golf course unlike the last time we're here. What an amazing improvement.
We didn't see any golf carts the last time we were here, now I saw quite a few of them, it's $16 per person but not many people are riding as I've seen because the golf course is quite walkable.

We came here for $26 golf sales, it’s now opened to public, I got the runaround to get to the place, directions guided to turn before Lockheed Martin entrance, the left entrance was block and the 2 guards were extremely hostile towards my mistake. So the only way to come in is from the front, the guards were nice here unlike the other 2.
The golf course was terrible even for $21, since I booked online, no $5 discount refunded. It’s ok, it’s still cheap until we teed off. Only walking since I’ve seen no carts anywhere. The greens were aired and sands only. The fairways are full of muds and not well kept.
So what makes a golf course great? Layout, fairways and greens, this golf course layout is ok, tons of dogleg right, left, the par 3s are mostly long. The whole golf course is about 6300 yards.
I’m not sure if I would come here again, for $33 with cart at Santa Clara is much better deal and the fairways are much nicer.<//Review>< Pictures>

<user_name>Peter Hey</user_name>< Pictures>
None<//Pictures>
<date>1493265164943< /date>< text>
This former military golf course inside Moffet Field has nice views of the adjacent SF bay as well as the large hangars next to the air strip. I haven't been here before the conversion to a public course, so can't really compare before and after, but the overall layout and maintenance is  still somewhat on the lower end of the scale for the bay area. Flat with lots of dog legs and only some bunker/water challenges. Reasonably priced and not so busy. To gain entry into Moffet Field to get to the golf course, you will have to show a picture ID. Right across from the club house is the Google parking lot for their fleet of "commuter buses" ... there's a lot of them.<//text>

Nice little new dog park the city of Ontario added on March 30th. It has 2 sections for large and small dogs, benches, a few obstacles, and a picnic table. Not as spacious as Dairyland dog park in Corona, but with grass, what more can you ask for.

You have to park in the Whispering Lake Golf Course parking lot and it’s just SW of the lot. Can’t miss it. Playful boxers, please come out to play with my Kala!< /Review>

More than 50% of the meat was dried enough you could not stick a fork into it because it was crumbling.   This was a HUGE oversight from the kitchen.   Again had to get hostess to find server...they did replace meal it was prepared properly and tasted good.    Again the flavor was not the issue......I might try later.</text>< pictures>
